The pizza was a great price for the area and the staff was very friendly and fast even on a Saturday night. We stopped here on the way to the sunset cliffs to watch the sunset and picnic with pizza I would definitely recommend it!! The only reason I'm giving it 4 stars is the pizza looked much better than it tasted. It was pretty meh, we did get the veggie so maybe the meat options are better! Overall I had a good experience here</Review>

<review>I might be biased but the pizza here reminds me of local pizza places growing up.

Pizza toppings are very generous! You get a lot of cheese, the sauce is slightly sweet & the crust isn't too thin or thick.

Also got the spaghetti here - could easily feed two people. Lots of sauce & comes with garlic bread. You can skip the side salad though... it's just iceberg lettuce with a couple of tomatoes.

Tip: the wait is about 15 minutes & there is no seat so call ahead :)<//review>< pics>

< Review>
Dr. Phillips is fantastic.  She cares, she doesn't rush through an appointment.   In my case, I came to her practice with several things I wanted to address.  She helped me be realistic and to prioritize what steps needs to be accomplished first.  My first appointment she ran significantly behind schedule.   Once you meet with her, you will understand why.   She isn't in and out in 10 minutes.  She takes time with you.   If she is doing that with everyone, then of course over the course of the day she is going to fall behind.   Bring a book, don't schedule something too close to your appointment or you will feel stressed.   From a back office perspective , the best thing about her practice is their use of the patient portal.   I can see my test results as soon as their posted, which means I can review them prior to my Dr. visit which allows me to get the most out of my appointment.  I can book, confirm, reschedule an appointment from the portal.  I travel for work and this ability to interact with her office on my time is incredibly valuable to me.   You will get your best experience with her practice if you have access to the internet and set up an account in their portal.  I've lived in Temecula/Murrieta for 5 years.   She is my 3rd Dr and I think my search is over.</Review>

<userid>110786099991326857884</userid>< name>

<time>1523471486927<//time>< Rating>
5< /Rating>
< Review>
Giving this five stars since the experience I had was really positive due to the people I was with, but I recognize that this isn't a 5-star hiking location for everyone:

There's a lot of hiking here. You can follow any one of many many many trails. This is great for people who want to re-visit over and over. This is less great for people like me who have a hard time understanding some of the signs placed at forks in the road. I honestly probably went the 'wrong' way a few times. Out of all the places I've ever hiked, this is one of the most likely for me to have gotten lost in.

Being close to San Francisco, when we started walking, under the thick evergreens, it was cold, damp, and dripping. And once we hiked above the initial layer of trees and the thin layer of fog, it was HOT (around 10am during the summer at this point). Going again, I would've worn a t-shirt and jeans.

The view of the city was predictably gray. We could see the Golden Gate Bridge peeking out, but not much inside the city.

Really lovely place, and right by the ocean too.< /Review>

<Review>Just north of San Francisco‚Äôs Golden Gate Bridge,¬†Mount Tamalpais State Park¬†rises majestically from the heart of Marin County. Its deep canyons and sweeping hillsides are cloaked with cool redwood forests, oak woodlands, open grasslands, and sturdy chaparral.

The¬†breathtaking panorama¬†from Mount Tamalpais‚Äôs 2,571-foot peak includes the Farallon Islands 25 miles out to sea, the Marin County hills, San Francisco Bay, the East Bay, and Mount Diablo. On rare occasions, the snow-covered Sierra Nevada can be seen 150 miles away.

The park offers superlative¬†hiking,¬†picnicking,¬†wildlife watching. Up top, a¬†visitor center¬†provides information, snacks, and souvenirs, and a ‚Äúgravity car barn‚Äù celebrates the old¬†Mount Tamalpais Scenic Railway. Down below, the 3,750-person capacity¬†Mountain Theater hosts outdoor plays and astronomy programs. Visitors may¬†camp¬†in several locations¬†or stay in¬†rustic view cabins¬†at Steep Ravine and (on private property) at West Point Inn.

Arrive early¬†to avoid heavy weekend and holiday traffic. Better yet, take the¬†West Marin Stage Coach.</Review><pics>None</pics><resp>None< /resp><GmapID>0x808591171b36502f:0x64161469a5add222< /GmapID></record>

< Review>
Easily accessible and highly trafficked. Good chance the trail will be busy on a nice day. Start from Pantoll (might be full parking if busy) if you only are interested in getting to the peak (half-day). Alternatively, starting at the steep ravine/dipsea trailhead(s) turns the peak summit into a full day hike (worth it!). Views from the top are fantastic if there are minimal fog/clouds rolling in from the bay.< /Review>
